ConcatPermissions(permissions ...[]Permission) []Permission {\n   372→\tif permissions == nil {\n   373→\t\treturn nil\n   374→\t}\n   375→\tperms := make([]Permission, 0)\n   376→\tfor _, p := range permissions {\n   377→\t\tpCopy := make([]Permission, 0, len(p))\n   378→\t\tcopy(pCopy, p)\n   379→\t\tperms = append(perms, p...)\n   380→\t}\n   381→\treturn perms\n   382→}\n   383→\n   384→// PrefixedRoleUID generates a uid from name with the same prefix.\n   385→// Generated uid is 28 bytes + length of prefix: <prefix>_base64(sha1(roleName))\n   386→func PrefixedRoleUID(roleName string) string {\n   387→\tprefix := strings.Split(roleName, \":\")[0] + \"_\"\n   388→\n   389→\t// #nosec G505 Used only for generating a 160 bit hash, it's not used for security purposes\n   390→\thasher := sha1.New()\n   391→\thasher.Write([]byte(roleName))\n   392→\n   393→\treturn fmt.Sprintf(\"%s%s\", prefix, base64.RawURLEncoding.EncodeToString(hasher.Sum(nil)))\n   394→}\n   395→\n   396→// ValidateFixedRole errors when a fixed role does not match expected pattern\n   397→func ValidateFixedRole(role RoleDTO) error {\n   398→\tif !strings.HasPrefix(role.Name, FixedRolePrefix) {\n   399→\t\treturn ErrFixedRolePrefixMissing\n   400→\t}\n   401→\treturn nil\n   402→}\n   403→\n   404→// ValidateBuiltInRoles errors when a built-in role does not match expected pattern\n   405→func ValidateBuiltInRoles(builtInRoles []string) error {\n   406→\tfor _, br := range builtInRoles {\n   407→\t\tif org.RoleType(br) == org.RoleNone {\n   408→\t\t\treturn ErrNoneRoleAssignment\n   409→\t\t}\n   410→\t\tif !org.RoleType(br).IsValid() && br != RoleGrafanaAdmin {\n   411→\t\t\treturn ErrInvalidBuiltinRole.Build(ErrInvalidBuiltinRoleData(br))\n   412→\t\t}\n   413→\t}\n   414→\treturn nil\n   415→}\n   416→\n   417→type RegistrationList struct {\n   418→\tmx            sync.RWMutex\n   419→\tregistrations []RoleRegistration\n   420→}\n   421→\n   422→func (m *RegistrationList) Append(regs ...RoleRegistration) {\n   423→\tm.mx.Lock()\n   424→\tdefer m.mx.Unlock()\n   425→\tm.registrations = append(m.registrations, regs...)\n   426→}\n   427→\n   428→func (m *RegistrationList) Range(f func(registration RoleRegistration) bool) {\n   429→\tm.mx.RLock()\n   430→\tdefer m.mx.RUnlock()\n   431→\tfor _, registration := range m.registrations {\n   432→\t\tif ok := f(registration); !ok {\n   433→\t\t\treturn\n   434→\t\t}\n   435→\t}\n   436→}\n   437→\n   438→func (m *RegistrationList) Slice() []RoleRegistration {\n   439→\tm.mx.RLock()\n   440→\tdefer m.mx.RUnlock()\n   441→\tout := make([]RoleRegistration, len(m.registrations))\n   442→\tcopy(out, m.registrations)\n   443→\treturn out\n   444→}\n   445→\n   446→func BuildBasicRoleDefinitions()
